<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-cantontimestampsecond"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.CantonTimestampSecond`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/CantonTimestampSecond.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class CantonTimestampSecond extends Ordered[CantonTimestampSecond] with Timestamp with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

A timestamp implementation for canton, which currently uses a LfTimestamp, which is rounded to the second.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-fulltransactionviewtree"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.FullTransactionViewTree`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/FullTransactionViewTree.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class FullTransactionViewTree extends TransactionViewTree with PrettyPrinting with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Wraps a GenTransactionTree where exactly one view (including subviews) is unblinded. The commonMetadata and participantMetadata are also unblinded. The submitterMetadata is unblinded if and only if the unblinded view is a root view.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-gentransactiontree"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.GenTransactionTree`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/GenTransactionTree.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class GenTransactionTree extends MerkleTreeInnerNode[GenTransactionTree] with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

A DAML transaction, decomposed into views (cf. ViewDecomposition) and embedded in a Merkle tree. Merkle tree nodes may or may not be blinded. This class is also used to represent transaction view trees and informee trees.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-lighttransactionviewtree"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.LightTransactionViewTree`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/LightTransactionViewTree.html)

**Signature**

```text
sealed abstract case class LightTransactionViewTree extends TransactionViewTree with HasProtocolVersionedWrapper[LightTransactionViewTree] with PrettyPrinting with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Wraps a GenTransactionTree where exactly one view is unblinded. The direct subviews of the unblinded view are blinded - this is why the class name is prefixed "Light".

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-merkleseq"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.MerkleSeq`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/MerkleSeq.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class MerkleSeq[+M <: VersionedMerkleTree[_]](rootOrEmpty: Option[MerkleTree[MerkleSeqElement[M]]])(representativeProtocolVersion: RepresentativeProtocolVersion[MerkleSeq.type], hashOps: HashOps) extends PrettyPrinting with HasProtocolVersionedWrapper[MerkleSeq[VersionedMerkleTree[_]]] with Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Wraps a sequence that is also a MerkleTree. Elements are arranged in a balanced binary tree. As a result, if all except one element are blinded, the resulting MerkleSeq has size logarithmic in the size of the fully unblinded MerkleSeq.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-merkletree"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.MerkleTree`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/MerkleTree.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait MerkleTree[+A] extends Product with Serializable with PrettyPrinting
```

**Summary**

Encapsulate a Merkle tree. Every node has an arbitrary number of children. Every node has a rootHash.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-merkletreeinnernode"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.MerkleTreeInnerNode`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/MerkleTreeInnerNode.html)

**Signature**

```text
abstract class MerkleTreeInnerNode[+A] extends MerkleTree[A]
```

**Summary**

An inner node of a Merkle tree. Has no data, no salt, and an arbitrary number of subtrees. An inner node is considered unblinded.

- Removed: -

**Signature**

```text
abstract class MerkleTreeLeaf[+A <: HasCryptographicEvidence] extends MerkleTree[A]
```

A leaf of a Merkle tree. Has data, a salt, and no children. A leaf is considered unblinded.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-data-peanoqueue"></a>

### `com.digitalasset.canton.data.PeanoQueue`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/PeanoQueue.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait PeanoQueue[K, V] extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

A Peano priority queue is a mutable priority queue of key-value pairs with ordered keys, starting from an index called the head, where pairs may be added in any order, but are polled strictly in their natural sequence. The order on keys must be a linear sequence, i.e., isomorphic to the order on a possibly unbounded interval of the integers. If the priority queue is missing a key from the sequence, we cannot poll that key until a key-value pair for that key is added.
